about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:</strong> This lecture explained
  how to specify exactly what is expected before a design process begins.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong>
  Olivier de Weck</p>

  <span m='4744790'>systems,</span> <span m='4745450'>when</span> <span m='4745630'>a</span>
  <span m='4745720'>higher</span> <span m='4746020'>level</span> <span m='4746350'>requirement</span>
